ago (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$syntax}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$options}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale from an other instance given to now


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int | array & {\em \$syntax} & if array passed, parameters will be extracted from it, the array may contains\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \textquotesingle{}syntax\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}parts\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}options\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} entry determines how to join multiple parts of the string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is a string, it\textquotesingle{}s used as a joiner glue } -\/ if \$join is a callable/closure, it get the list of string and should return a string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is an array, the first item will be the default glue, and the second item } will be used instead of the glue for the last item ` -\/ if \$join is true, it will be guessed from the locale (\textquotesingle{}list' translation file entry) \`{} -\/ if \$join is missing, a space will be used as glue if int passed, it add modifiers\+: Possible values\+:
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE no modifiers
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+NOW add ago/from now modifier
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+OTHER add before/after modifier Default value\+: Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & maximum number of parts to display (default value\+: 1\+: single part) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$options} & human diff options\\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_abe78ec271a838068d614b7d2fdc756de} 
create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$year}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{\$month}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$day}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$hour}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{\$minute}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{\$second}{ = {\ttfamily 0}, }\item[{}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a new Carbon instance from a specific date and time.

If any of \$year, \$month or \$day are set to null their now() values will be used.

If \$hour is null it will be set to its now() value and the default values for \$minute and \$second will be their now() values.

If \$hour is not null then the default values for \$minute and \$second will be 0.

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a04561f8b72cbf657321ab0cb065904bc}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!createSafe@{createSafe}}
\index{createSafe@{createSafe}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createSafe()}{createSafe()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a04561f8b72cbf657321ab0cb065904bc} 
create\+Safe (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$year}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$month}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$day}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$hour}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$minute}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$second}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a new safe Carbon instance from a specific date and time.

If any of \$year, \$month or \$day are set to null their now() values will be used.

If \$hour is null it will be set to its now() value and the default values for \$minute and \$second will be their now() values.

If \$hour is not null then the default values for \$minute and \$second will be 0.

If one of the set values is not valid, an Invalid\+Date\+Exception will be thrown.

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a7aa8aebb0e289fc646d44a8fe49cb251}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!from@{from}}
\index{from@{from}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{from()}{from()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a7aa8aebb0e289fc646d44a8fe49cb251} 
from (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$other}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$syntax}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$options}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

@alias diff\+For\+Humans

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale from current instance to an other instance given (or now if null given).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
Carbon | \textbackslash{}\+Date\+Time\+Interface | string | array | null & {\em \$other} & if array passed, will be used as parameters array, see \$syntax below; if null passed, now will be used as comparison reference; if any other type, it will be converted to date and used as reference. \\
\hline
int | array & {\em \$syntax} & if array passed, parameters will be extracted from it, the array may contains\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \textquotesingle{}syntax\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}parts\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}options\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} entry determines how to join multiple parts of the string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is a string, it\textquotesingle{}s used as a joiner glue } -\/ if \$join is a callable/closure, it get the list of string and should return a string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is an array, the first item will be the default glue, and the second item } will be used instead of the glue for the last item ` -\/ if \$join is true, it will be guessed from the locale (\textquotesingle{}list' translation file entry) ` -\/ if \$join is missing, a space will be used as glue
\item \textquotesingle{}other' entry (see above) if int passed, it add modifiers\+: Possible values\+:
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE no modifiers
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+NOW add ago/from now modifier
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+OTHER add before/after modifier Default value\+: Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & maximum number of parts to display (default value\+: 1\+: single unit) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$options} & human diff options\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a29faa12aa7b4a9c5788241d2c47d84d3}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!getOffsetString@{getOffsetString}}
\index{getOffsetString@{getOffsetString}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getOffsetString()}{getOffsetString()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a29faa12aa7b4a9c5788241d2c47d84d3} 
get\+Offset\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{string}]{\$separator}{ = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\+:\textquotesingle{}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the offset hour and minute formatted with +/-\/ and a given separator ("{}\+:"{} by default). For example, if the time zone is 9 hours 30 minutes, you\textquotesingle{}ll get "{}+09\+:30"{}, with "{}@@"{} as first argument, "{}+09@@30"{}, with "{}"{} as first argument, "{}+0930"{}. Negative offset will return something like "{}-\/12\+:00"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$separator} & string to place between hours and minutes ("{}\+:"{} by default) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a367a13a6823265806ad15a89e78f29dc} 
make (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$var}{, }\item[{Date\+Time\+Zone\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}null}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Make a Carbon instance from given variable if possible.

Always return a new instance. Parse only strings and only these likely to be dates (skip intervals and recurrences). Throw an exception for invalid format, but otherwise return null.

parse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Date\+Time\+Interface\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_afe4a91ea06cbf76a0a97581cef0f8759}{Week\+Day}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3c6c2c22a96bdc8eae207fe0230d92a7}{Month}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3a759da26a0e7e7b22a85dddef939c05}{int}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}float\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}null}]{\$time}{, }\item[{Date\+Time\+Zone\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3a759da26a0e7e7b22a85dddef939c05}{int}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}null}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a carbon instance from a string.

This is an alias for the constructor that allows better fluent syntax as it allows you to do Carbon\+::parse(\textquotesingle{}Monday next week\textquotesingle{})-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}fn() rather than (new Carbon(\textquotesingle{}Monday next week\textquotesingle{}))-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}fn().

raw\+Parse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Date\+Time\+Interface\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_afe4a91ea06cbf76a0a97581cef0f8759}{Week\+Day}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3c6c2c22a96bdc8eae207fe0230d92a7}{Month}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3a759da26a0e7e7b22a85dddef939c05}{int}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}float\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}null}]{\$time}{, }\item[{Date\+Time\+Zone\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3a759da26a0e7e7b22a85dddef939c05}{int}}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}null}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Create a carbon instance from a string.

This is an alias for the constructor that allows better fluent syntax as it allows you to do Carbon\+::parse(\textquotesingle{}Monday next week\textquotesingle{})-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}fn() rather than (new Carbon(\textquotesingle{}Monday next week\textquotesingle{}))-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}fn().

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a2bd2cddec1c6e4865fcd21f1781844dd}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!setTestNow@{setTestNow}}
\index{setTestNow@{setTestNow}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTestNow()}{setTestNow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a2bd2cddec1c6e4865fcd21f1781844dd} 
set\+Test\+Now (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{mixed}]{\$test\+Now}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Set a Carbon instance (real or mock) to be returned when a "{}now"{} instance is created. The provided instance will be returned specifically under the following conditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A call to the static now() method, ex. \doxylink{interface_psr_1_1_clock_1_1_clock_interface_a80593ccdc0339775ddd5d82c37ca4f6b}{Carbon\textbackslash{}now()}
\item When a null (or blank string) is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon(null)}
\item When the string "{}now"{} is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new Carbon(\textquotesingle{}now\textquotesingle{})
\item When a string containing the desired time is passed to Carbon\+::parse().
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note the timezone parameter was left out of the examples above and has no affect as the mock value will be returned regardless of its value.

Only the moment is mocked with set\+Test\+Now(), the timezone will still be the one passed as parameter of date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+get() as a fallback (see set\+Test\+Now\+And\+Timezone()).

To clear the test instance call this method using the default parameter of null.

/!\textbackslash{} Use this method for unit tests only.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
Date\+Time\+Interface | Closure | static | string | false | null & {\em \$test\+Now} & real or mock Carbon instance \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a3ef352f2f0760e443f3c213cb0b4cbef}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!setTestNowAndTimezone@{setTestNowAndTimezone}}
\index{setTestNowAndTimezone@{setTestNowAndTimezone}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTestNowAndTimezone()}{setTestNowAndTimezone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a3ef352f2f0760e443f3c213cb0b4cbef} 
set\+Test\+Now\+And\+Timezone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$test\+Now}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$timezone}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Set a Carbon instance (real or mock) to be returned when a "{}now"{} instance is created. The provided instance will be returned specifically under the following conditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A call to the static now() method, ex. \doxylink{interface_psr_1_1_clock_1_1_clock_interface_a80593ccdc0339775ddd5d82c37ca4f6b}{Carbon\textbackslash{}now()}
\item When a null (or blank string) is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new \doxylink{namespace_carbon}{Carbon(null)}
\item When the string "{}now"{} is passed to the constructor or parse(), ex. new Carbon(\textquotesingle{}now\textquotesingle{})
\item When a string containing the desired time is passed to Carbon\+::parse().
\end{DoxyItemize}

It will also align default timezone (e.\+g. call date\+\_\+default\+\_\+timezone\+\_\+set()) with the second argument or if null, with the timezone of the given date object.

To clear the test instance call this method using the default parameter of null.

/!\textbackslash{} Use this method for unit tests only.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
Date\+Time\+Interface | Closure | static | string | false | null & {\em \$test\+Now} & real or mock Carbon instance \\

\end{DoxyParams}

timezone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Date\+Time\+Zone\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_carbon_a3a759da26a0e7e7b22a85dddef939c05}{int}}}]{\$value}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

@alias set\+Timezone \Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_ade4cef9152b6ef34bafde82704817ba7}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!to@{to}}
\index{to@{to}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to()}{to()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_ade4cef9152b6ef34bafde82704817ba7} 
to (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$other}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$syntax}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$options}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale from an other instance given (or now if null given) to current instance.

When comparing a value in the past to default now\+: 1 hour from now 5 months from now

When comparing a value in the future to default now\+: 1 hour ago 5 months ago

When comparing a value in the past to another value\+: 1 hour after 5 months after

When comparing a value in the future to another value\+: 1 hour before 5 months before


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
Carbon | \textbackslash{}\+Date\+Time\+Interface | string | array | null & {\em \$other} & if array passed, will be used as parameters array, see \$syntax below; if null passed, now will be used as comparison reference; if any other type, it will be converted to date and used as reference. \\
\hline
int | array & {\em \$syntax} & if array passed, parameters will be extracted from it, the array may contains\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \textquotesingle{}syntax\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}parts\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}options\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} entry determines how to join multiple parts of the string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is a string, it\textquotesingle{}s used as a joiner glue } -\/ if \$join is a callable/closure, it get the list of string and should return a string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is an array, the first item will be the default glue, and the second item } will be used instead of the glue for the last item ` -\/ if \$join is true, it will be guessed from the locale (\textquotesingle{}list' translation file entry) ` -\/ if \$join is missing, a space will be used as glue
\item \textquotesingle{}other' entry (see above) if int passed, it add modifiers\+: Possible values\+:
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE no modifiers
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+NOW add ago/from now modifier
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+OTHER add before/after modifier Default value\+: Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & maximum number of parts to display (default value\+: 1\+: single unit) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$options} & human diff options\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_af064e0ee897217137f41d927367d9ccc}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!toNow@{toNow}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{toNow()}{toNow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_af064e0ee897217137f41d927367d9ccc} 
to\+Now (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$syntax}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$options}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale from an other instance given to now


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int | array & {\em \$syntax} & if array passed, parameters will be extracted from it, the array may contains\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \textquotesingle{}syntax\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}parts\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}options\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} entry determines how to join multiple parts of the string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is a string, it\textquotesingle{}s used as a joiner glue } -\/ if \$join is a callable/closure, it get the list of string and should return a string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is an array, the first item will be the default glue, and the second item } will be used instead of the glue for the last item ` -\/ if \$join is true, it will be guessed from the locale (\textquotesingle{}list' translation file entry) \`{} -\/ if \$join is missing, a space will be used as glue if int passed, it add modifiers\+: Possible values\+:
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE no modifiers
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+NOW add ago/from now modifier
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+OTHER add before/after modifier Default value\+: Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & maximum number of parts to display (default value\+: 1\+: single part) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$options} & human diff options\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a0e51c4f6cb49a13ffdab5f92e5835fac}\index{CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}!until@{until}}
\index{until@{until}!CarbonInterface@{CarbonInterface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{until()}{until()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{interface_carbon_1_1_carbon_interface_a0e51c4f6cb49a13ffdab5f92e5835fac} 
until (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$other}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$syntax}{ = {\ttfamily null}, }\item[{}]{\$short}{ = {\ttfamily false}, }\item[{}]{\$parts}{ = {\ttfamily 1}, }\item[{}]{\$options}{ = {\ttfamily null}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

@alias to

Get the difference in a human readable format in the current locale from an other instance given (or now if null given) to current instance.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
Carbon | \textbackslash{}\+Date\+Time\+Interface | string | array | null & {\em \$other} & if array passed, will be used as parameters array, see \$syntax below; if null passed, now will be used as comparison reference; if any other type, it will be converted to date and used as reference. \\
\hline
int | array & {\em \$syntax} & if array passed, parameters will be extracted from it, the array may contains\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \textquotesingle{}syntax\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}short\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}parts\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}options\textquotesingle{} entry (see below)
\item \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} entry determines how to join multiple parts of the string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is a string, it\textquotesingle{}s used as a joiner glue } -\/ if \$join is a callable/closure, it get the list of string and should return a string {\ttfamily  -\/ if \$join is an array, the first item will be the default glue, and the second item } will be used instead of the glue for the last item ` -\/ if \$join is true, it will be guessed from the locale (\textquotesingle{}list' translation file entry) ` -\/ if \$join is missing, a space will be used as glue
\item \textquotesingle{}other' entry (see above) if int passed, it add modifiers\+: Possible values\+:
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE no modifiers
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+NOW add ago/from now modifier
\item Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+RELATIVE\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+OTHER add before/after modifier Default value\+: Carbon\+Interface\+::\+DIFF\+\_\+\+ABSOLUTE 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
bool & {\em \$short} & displays short format of time units \\
\hline
int & {\em \$parts} & maximum number of parts to display (default value\+: 1\+: single unit) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$options} & human diff options\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
string 
\end{DoxyReturn}
